focus_tree = {

	id = italy_focus

	country = {
		factor = 0
		modifier = {
			tag = ITA
			add = 20
		}
	}

##SICK MAN OF EUROPE

	focus = {
		id = ITA_divided_nation
		icon = The_sick_man_of_Europe
		x = 15
		y = 0
		cost = 1

		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_divided_nation"
			custom_effect_tooltip = list_of_statalist_parties_TT
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 80
		}
	}

##DIPLOMATIC FOCUS##

	focus = {
		id = ITA_diplomatic_focus
		icon = improve_relations
		x = 115
		y = 0
		cost = 1

		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL FOCUS_FILTER_NATO}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_diplomatic_focus"
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = ITA_abandon_the_west
		icon = attack_nato
		relative_position_id = ITA_diplomatic_focus
		x = -2
		y = 1
		cost = 10

		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_NATO FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL }

		prerequisite = {
			focus = ITA_diplomatic_focus
		}

		available = {
			threat > 0.15
			has_idea = NATO_member
		}
		cancel_if_invalid = yes

		mutually_exclusive = {
			focus = ITA_strenghten_ties_with_west
		}

		bypass = {
			NOT = { has_idea = NATO_member }
		}

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_abandon_the_west"
			NATO_leave = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_east_aligned_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_west_aligned_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

	focus = {
		id = ITA_strenghten_ties_with_west
		icon = align_to_nato
		relative_position_id = ITA_diplomatic_focus
		x = 2
		y = 1
		cost = 5

		search_filters = {FOCUS_FILTER_NATO FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL}

		prerequisite = {
			focus = ITA_diplomatic_focus

			focus = ITA_abandon_the_west
		}

		available = {
			threat > 0.15
			has_idea = NATO_member
		}
		cancel_if_invalid = yes

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_strenghten_ties_with_west"
			add_political_power = 50
			every_country = {
				limit = { has_idea = NATO_member }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = reaffirmed_NATO }
				reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = reaffirmed_NATO }
			}
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				has_east_aligned_government = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_west_aligned_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

				add_opinion_modifier = {

					modifier = declaration_of_friendship
				}
				set_country_flag = ITA_friendship_focus
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 1 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ROOT.id }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS.id }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 1 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = SOV.id }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = THIS.id }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 40
				OR = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 }
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 20 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

			set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }

		}

			factor = 80

				factor = 16

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = party_pop_array^16
				always = yes
			}
		}

		}
		cancel_if_invalid = yes

		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus ITA_repeal_former_government_measures_6"
			allow_elections = yes
			add_political_power = -500
			set_country_flag = dynamic_flag
			set_country_flag = ITA_restored_democracy
			clr_country_flag = ITA_undemocratic_coup
			remove_ideas = ITA_parliament_dismantled
			clr_country_flag = ITA_romanization_decisions
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = ITA_peaceful_takeovers }
					remove_ideas = {
						ITA_peaceful_takeovers
						ITA_economic_freedoms
					}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = ITA_divide_et_impera }
					remove_ideas = {
						ITA_divide_et_impera
						ITA_war_economy_spirit
						Planned_Economy_ITA
						ITA_party_propaganda
					}
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = md_closed_economy
						add_idea = consumption_economy
					}
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_party_propaganda_modifier }
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ITA_party_popularity_drift_modifier }
			set_temp_variable = { drift_switch_change = 0.1 }
			modify_reform_expectance_effect = yes
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = ITA_migrants_from_africa_limited
				add_idea = ITA_migrants_from_africa
			}

				can_create_factions = no
			}
		}

			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 80
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 15 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
